The Strategy for Resolving Bandit-Puppet Problems 195

— Me

Regarding the recent Sino-Japanese negotiations, I have repeatedly stated that assuming that negotiations are conducted while constantly being invaded by bandits and puppets, such negotiations are not only ineffective but also fall into the trap of bandit-puppet schemes. It is better to stop the negotiations immediately. Regarding the bandit disaster in Suiyuan, I have also contributed some opinions, saying that in the bandit suppression plan, not only should our people provide a steady stream of supplies, but our authorities should also provide as much assistance as possible in terms of strength. This principle is obviously clear, and it does not require knowledgeable people to foresee it.

Now the Suiyuan incident has escalated to a serious level, and the war is in full swing. According to the Taiyuan telegram on the 17th, our frontline soldiers are fighting bravely in the icy and snowy weather, repeatedly thwarting the enemy's offensive. Our brave frontline soldiers are able to embrace this greatest determination, not hesitating to make any sacrifice to fight for the survival of the nation and protect the territory of the country. This spirit naturally deserves our admiration. As for the material supply in the rear, our people across the country are uniting to launch a Suiyuan support movement. Our military authorities must have already considered the assistance in terms of strength, so it is unnecessary for us to worry about it again.

What I want to say now is that more careful consideration should be given to the strategic direction of bandit suppression. According to our ancient military strategists, the momentum of offense and defense is different, and the emotions of labor and leisure are different. In war, it seems that it is easier to defend and more difficult to attack, and the attacker labors while the defender rests. This statement originally refers to situations where the strengths of both sides are equal. In the current era of scientific and mechanical warfare, it is not appropriate to adhere to this statement. Now the bandit army is attacking Suiyuan, using aircraft and artillery as cover. If we do not have these two, or if we have them but their strength is not equal, then no matter how much we defend, it will be difficult to sustain, and there will only be sacrifices, making it difficult to defeat the enemy. Sitting and defending a dangerous city will not help the facts. This is the first unacceptable thing.

Therefore, the art of war says that whoever strikes first controls the enemy, and whoever strikes later is controlled by the enemy. Now the situation in Suiyuan is that we are controlled by others everywhere. Using the method of responding to attacks to defend is not a long-term solution, and the enemy concentrates its heavy troops in one place, so no matter how we resist, we will always expend more effort and achieve less success. We should change our strategy, send out a force like horns to divide their strength, and use the method of creating a diversion to confuse their vision, and then the great enemy can be eliminated. Moreover, the bandit-puppet army has occupied quite a bit of our land, and if we do not resolve this completely at this time, when will we wait? We can no longer stick to the saying that "if people do not offend me, I will not offend them," and sit and suffer the trampling of the bandit-puppets.

Page 20

Now the bandit-puppet army's strategy is to concentrate its main force on Shangdu on one side and Guo Zhong on Bailing Temple on the other, advancing and attacking separately. They can attack and defend. We only have the means to protect ourselves and no strategy for offense. Nothing is worse than this loss of planning. Even if Suiyuan is fortunately preserved, it will not compensate for the broken territory outside the customs. If Suiyuan fails, the provinces of Shanxi, Shaanxi, and Gansu will be in danger of losing their lips and teeth. Therefore, in my opinion, the plan to defend only one corner is definitely not the best plan.

Gourd 196

— Liao Chuxiu

In front of my residence, there is an old-fashioned house. In the spring, a vine climbed onto the roof tiles. In the summer, small white flowers bloomed, and in early autumn, fruits grew—two "gourds."

The "Gourd Flower Mirror" records: also known as bottle gourd, sown in the first or second month, it sprouts and climbs, its leaves resembling winter melon but slightly rounder, with soft hairs, white flowers bloom in May or June, the fruit is initially white, and turns yellow after frost. One type, round and large, is called "bao" [饱, full]. It is also named "hu" [孤, solitary], because it can hold water like a bubble. It can also be used as a container for storing wine. Another type, large at the bottom and small at the top, with a thin waist and a narrow mouth, is called "gourd." It can hold medicinal pills, large ones can be used as jar lids, small ones can be used as wine cups, children use them to float in water, and musicians use them to make sheng [笙, a reed pipe wind instrument].

In the countryside, there probably aren't many children who haven't played with gourds in their childhood. When I was young, I loved gourds very much. However, this was limited to the "large at the bottom and small at the top, with a thin waist and a narrow mouth" type. I used a red lacquered rope to hang it on my body. Later, after reading mythological books like "The Investiture of the Gods," I learned that immortals carried a gourd with them, and I loved it even more.

As for the "round and large" type, I have disliked it since I was little. My dislike for it is not because of the gourd itself, but because I dislike the shiny heads of monks. "Gourd, gourd head," I then associate and dislike this "round and large" type of bottle gourd.

Although I disliked it very much, my family still planted this "bottle gourd" every year. Between summer and autumn, small green bottle gourds grew on the vines. I secretly used a sharp nail to break them one by one. Only the ones that were too high to reach were allowed to grow.

In winter, the ladles in the rice jar and water jar were all unusable. My mother would tell people to pick the grown bottle gourds. They would be carefully split open, the seeds and pulp removed, to replace the broken ones. But at that time, I didn't dislike it any less because it was useful. Sometimes, behind my mother's back, I would put the bottle gourd from the rice jar and water jar on the ground and stomp on it forcefully.

I don't remember how old I was. My cousin came to my house to play. He brought a sheng [笙] made of "gourd," playing it with a "woo woo" sound. I was very happy to see it, but I didn't ask him for it, because I knew it would be useless even if I asked. Later that night, I deliberately stayed up very late, asking the servant to bring me my cousin's gourd sheng [笙] to play. I blew it for a long time, but it didn't make a sound. So I became very angry, feeling that this gourd was also deceiving me, and I stomped on it.

After stomping on it, I was very worried. I was afraid that my cousin would suddenly remember his gourd. But strangely, he never thought about it again, while I secretly hid all my own gourds, afraid that he would see them and be reminded of his own.

From then on, I no longer played with gourds.

When I was a little older, I regretted the story of destroying bottle gourds in my childhood. But it was too late.

In Zhuangzi's "Free and Easy Wandering," Huizi said to Zhuangzi: "The King of Wei gave me seeds of a large gourd, and I planted them and it yielded five bushels of water. If I filled it with water, it would be too heavy to lift. If I cut it in half to make a ladle, it would be so large that it wouldn't fit anywhere. It's not that it's not big, but I smashed it because it was useless." Zhuangzi said: "You are truly inept at using things... Now that you have a five-bushel gourd, why not consider using it as a large boat to float on the rivers and lakes? Worrying that it's too large and won't fit anywhere shows that you still have a closed mind!"

This is naturally a fable, but I truly felt for the first time the great usefulness of the bottle gourd. Whenever I had the opportunity to see a bottle gourd, I would always ponder for a long time.

Naturally, I still have a closed mind! Although I ponder because of the great usefulness of the bottle gourd, I still can't help but frown at the appearance of the bottle gourd.

The "Supplementary Records of Yijian" says, "Zhao Gongheng, a member of the imperial family, lived in Xiuzhou. He was easygoing and good at being considerate to others, but he was naturally humorous. Whenever he could crack a smile, he would blurt it out. Everyone who saw him respected and feared him. Because he had little hair, people commonly called him 'Zhao Gourd.'" Gong Jinglu wrote in "Reduced Character Magnolia," "Family is rarely amiss, raised a branch drawn in the same way; good for nothing, only to entangle the inverted vines by the fence, several times on the water, pressing and rubbing a hundred times is truly strong; nowhere to accommodate him, just let him bake in the hot sun into a dried knot." Then, I feel that the laughableness of the gourd head is definitely not limited to me alone. I am here just using it to make light of myself.

"If this child were fifteen years old, my whole life of hardship would be over!" thought the mother.

— Written by Hu Kao

At the Character Analysis Stall 197

— Luo Jia

Sanzi took advantage of the boss's wife asking him to pick up the little boss from school and secretly slipped into the alley in front. He anxiously looked around before sitting down at the side of Sai Tieko's character analysis stall, carefully taking out three crumpled pieces of letter paper and an envelope from his inner pocket. —He had stolen these things from the store half a month ago and had been keeping them treasured ever since, but only today did he get the chance to let these papers see the light of day again.

Sai Tieko raised his reading glasses and sized up his customer before taking the letter paper and envelope from Sanzi, spreading them out and holding them down with an inkstone.

"Tell me! Who are you writing to? What are you writing?..." Sai Tieko folded the paper, ground the ink, and bit on the tip of his brush as he asked Sanzi.

"I'm writing to..." Sanzi said hesitantly, looking around. "I'm writing to my grandmother, sir! Please tell her that I'm in Shanghai, at Huang Jinlong's cigarette paper shop. I get up before dawn—really before dawn, even earlier than when Grandmother gets up in the countryside. Hongquan wakes me up. That shop assistant, Hongquan, is the shop assistant who started working at the store before me. Sir! Please tell her that I go to sleep very, very late, so I'm sleepy all day long..."

"Not getting enough sleep is the hardest, sir."

"It's been several days since the tenth lunar month," please tell her, sir. "I broke a wine bottle belonging to the boss's wife. It was a cheap bottle, like the soy sauce bottles that are placed in the corner of Chen Deye's kitchen. Because I got up too early in the morning, I accidentally broke it. The boss's wife wants me to pay for it, but I don't have any money to pay her. The two hundred cash that Grandmother gave me when I left home is all gone. So I received two hard slaps from the boss's wife..."

"I cried for a long time. I miss Grandmother."

"The two hundred cash that Grandmother gave me, I've spent it all. I didn't waste it, I really had no choice. Hongquan, that shop assistant, he knew I had two hundred cash, and he wanted me to treat him, otherwise, he wouldn't teach me how to do things. So I treated him to eight copper coins worth of peanuts. And once, the little boss wanted me to buy him candy, otherwise he would tell the boss's wife and I would get beaten. I have four copper coins left, and I bought an old rooster made of mud. It makes a sound when you blow it. I'm keeping it hidden, and I haven't broken it at all. I'll bring it back for my little brother when I go home."

"I... you... also got slapped twice by the boss's wife, and I hurt my head a little. It hurts a lot, it still hurts now. But it wasn't my fault, because the master told me to carry a package of toilet paper, and I didn't hear the boss's wife calling me from upstairs."

"Please tell my grandmother, sir! Please don't worry, if the boss's wife doesn't beat me, I'll be fine!"

"Please tell my grandmother, sir! I miss her very much. Because I miss her, I often cry. Please don't worry, Grandmother, I won't be naughty anymore. From now on, I'll listen to Grandmother in everything, and I won't upset her anymore!"

"It would be so good if I could go back to Grandmother's side! Sir, please tell her that I'm not naughty like I used to be at all! I miss Grandmother!"

"...Oh! And! Sir! There's also a spinning top, I left it in the wooden box under my bed when I left. Just give it to my little brother. I don't want it anymore."

Sai Tieko began to write on the letter paper, "To my dear Grandmother." Nine characters, with the brush held in his mouth, he stopped writing and kept looking at his customer.

"So, where is this letter going to be sent to?"

"Sent to the countryside. At Chen Street Town, West Market End, Chen Deye will pass it on to Grandmother."

"What countryside is that?"

"It's in the countryside. It's called Chen Family Town. Chen Deye is very famous. He lives on the east side of the Zhang Family Residence, that big house. Just give this letter to my grandmother, that Shi Grandmother who stokes the fire, or say Sanzi's grandmother, they won't make a mistake..."

"You can't write it like that on a letter!" Sai Tieko was embarrassed by him.

"Just write it like that, sir! They won't make a mistake. Sir, please tell my grandmother, sir, I miss her!"

Tragedy in the Dusk 198

— Lan Pei

At dusk, I watched the sunset from the deck. Several seagulls following the ship soared around, their simple and sincere language adding infinite vitality to the picturesque and poetic twilight.

Only then did I realize the moving power of "beauty"—extending to all kinds of creatures. Who can say that the birds aren't in love with the dusk?

Look! On the golden and brilliant sea surface of the setting sun, in the beautiful twilight glow—in the poetic realm where the clear wind whispers from the seabed: more than a dozen passionate birds soar! Who can sing this poem?

One day—a tragedy occurred.

Perhaps it was due to the magnificent allure of the setting sun. Perhaps it was...—a bird flew far away from the flock towards the place where the sun was setting. Like an arrow, like a gust of wind, it flew so fast!

We all became worried, how would it come back?

However, it came back. Exhausted and frantically flapping its wings, it staggered back.

—It's back—

Amidst sympathetic cheers, but—it couldn't hold on in the end. It looked so weak, suddenly, it almost fell into the sea. It flew low over the sea, struggling desperately. The waves splashed, wetting its chest—abdomen. It struggled once, twice—rising up, finally: exhausted! Let a wave carry it into the deep seabed!

We silently stared at the sea for a moment. An indescribable feeling permeated our hearts.

Night clouds rose from the horizon.

China and West (1040) Afternoon 1:00 to 1:45

Opening "Lin Chushi"

A corner of Lonely Mountain on the lake is green. Three hundred varieties of plum blossoms form a forest. What a, Lin Bu, whose heart is indifferent and far away. He is content with a bamboo thatched hut. He is not tainted by even a bit of dust. Not only does he love learning and never seek office. Moreover, for twenty years, his feet have not stepped into the city. Plum blossoms are his wife and his son is a crane. It can be seen that his unyielding heart and proud bones are innate. When the weather is cold, the crane guards the plum blossoms. It seems that Xuan Shi is carrying on the filial love and there are still a thousand affections. The plum is like a beautiful cheek. The crane cries in the shade. One is, a fairy from Guye Mountain smiling prettily. One is, the clear and light chick phoenix reading aloud. Occasionally, a distinguished guest visits the mountain temple. His servant lets the phoenix fly into the blue clouds. Only see them dancing gracefully to welcome the head of the family. The gentleman is, on a small boat with a melon rind returning home from afar. Better than the innocent children of the Tao family waiting at the brushwood gate. He is skilled in calligraphy and painting. Loves to sing and write poetry. Saying that I don't need fame in the world, so stop saving the drafts. However, sparse shadows slant across the clear and shallow water. Faint fragrance floats in the yellow dusk moon. It has already been a beautiful sentence passed down to this day. Afterwards, the king awarded grain and silk. He also changed his name to He Qinghao, Mr. Gaojie, leaving a unique name behind him. It is said that Maoling will one day seek the lost drafts. Fortunately, there were no Fengshan articles. It can be seen even more that Feng Liu is dissolute and has long neglected Zhang Qing.

Opening "Yingying's Heart of Qin"

The fragrance of lotus and the clear water move in the cool breeze. The water moves, the cool breeze extends the summer day. Long days of summer. The fragrance of green lotus. Miss Yingying calls Hongniang. With you in the fragrant boudoir, there is nothing to do. Go to the back garden to relieve boredom and dispel your worries. Hongniang listens. Joyously. Following the young lady, she moves her steps downstairs. Turning and winding, she faces inward. She passes through the wooden fragrant shed behind the bamboo screen. She walks to the White Plum Pavilion and stands. There, she sees that it is densely shaded from the sun. What a clever little Hongniang. She hurriedly pushes open the windows on all four sides. The table is placed in the center. The Yaoqin [a stringed instrument] is taken out of its bag. Incense is burned in the precious tripod furnace. The young lady sits down and starts playing. First, she plays "The Lament of Xiangfei." Then she plays "The Phoenix Seeks the Male." When several Yaoqin songs are finished, she sees that the golden crow is gradually setting in the west. Hongniang is busy and flustered. She closes the windows on all four sides. The Yaoqin is hung on the wall. The smoke and fragrance are extinguished in the precious tripod furnace. The mistress and maid return to the boudoir together. Going forward along the original road. The small bridge winds and reflects in the pond. She sees two mandarin ducks resting and playing in the pond. The servant girl is frightened. The cool breeze of early summer moves the water. The water moves, and the cool breeze extends the summer. Although the beautiful scenery is unusual.

Movies

Public Performance of "Sai Jinhua" 202

The tragic life of Sai Jinhua is now being brought to the stage, which is truly an unprecedented treat for the eyes of those who love theater. The performers are the 40's Society, based on Xia Yan's original work. The content is grand and moving. There are grand scenes such as Sai Jinhua persuading Waldersee and others when the Eight-Nation Alliance invaded Beijing 37 years ago, which are worthy of singing and weeping about. The stage and screen actress Wang Ying plays Sai Jinhua, performing vividly and colorfully. The section where Sai Jinhua is old and faded, with a tragic ending, is guaranteed to bring tears to people's eyes. There are more than 60 performers, all well-known figures on the stage and silver screen. The directors are Hong Shen, Shi Dongshan, Ying Yunwei, Ouyang Yuqian and others. Such a large gathering of talent is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity. Public performance at the Jincheng Grand Theater starting today.

Lili Li in "The Bleeding Record of Wolf Mountain" 203

The Glory of Domestic Films - "Shanghai" to Show "Night of Revelry" 204

A Valuable Piece of News:

The humorous comedy "Night of Revelry" directed by Shi Dongshan of Xinhua Company has been scheduled to be shown at the Shanghai Grand Theater, which has never shown Chinese films before, starting on the 21st of this month (Saturday).

The script for "Night of Revelry" is adapted from the famous stage work "The Inspector General" by the great Russian writer Gogol. After watching this film, the Soviet ambassador praised the film's achievements and requested that the company allow the film to be shown in the Soviet Union, and the owner of the Shanghai Grand Theater took this opportunity and asked someone to entrust the film to Xinhua so that the film could be shown in the theater first, and he also found a way to explain it to the side.

The fact that "Night of Revelry" can be shown at the Shanghai Grand Theater, and even exported to the Soviet Union, allows us to imagine the value of this film. At the same time, we are very pleased that domestic films can have the opportunity to be introduced to domestic audiences, and cause them to pay attention to Chinese films.

Leah Stehlin and Leslie Rogers in "Endless Romance" 205

Grand Light Shows "Riding the Dragon and Praising the Phoenix" 206

Starring Clark Gable and Myrna Loy

Clark Gable is the number one celebrity in Hollywood. Myrna Loy is a famous star who has been famous for a long time. Their collaboration, "Cain and Mabel," will be shown at the Grand Light today. The story tells of a pair of sworn enemies who, because of the theater publicist's publicity trick, unintentionally turn from enemies into relatives. "Hating them to the point of grinding your teeth, and loving them to the point of treasuring your heart," these two sentences are no different from a portrayal of the characters in the play. Not only is the plot and performance of this film hot and extreme, but the grandeur of the song and dance scenes is unprecedented. The mountains are high and reach into the clouds, the pearl light is brilliant, the flesh screen stands tall, and the spring colors are endless. I am afraid that only Warner Bros. has such courage and is willing to make such sacrifices.
